2 major issues

Actual calculations:

251.32+321.44+269.1 = 841.86 (subtotal)

Discounts = 128.8+164.74+137.91 = 431.45

Total (after discount applied) = 841.86-431.45 = 410.41

Minicart issue:

subtotal displayed here is incorrect

cart summary

Pradeep Agnihotri
August 20, 2020, 11:23 PM

The subtotal issue was caused due to BorderFree replacing it with the calculated order total. This has been resolved in https://borngroup.atlassian.net/browse/DBI-5038 .

The issue with alignment of the currency is being tracked in https://borngroup.atlassian.net/browse/DBI-5044 .

Hence please close this ticket since both the reported issues are being handled in separate tickets.
